Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

022233,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
022234,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
022235,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
022236,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
022237,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
022238,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
022239,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
022240,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
022241,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
022242,000011:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
022243,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
022244,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
022245,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 504-623
022246,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
022247,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
022248,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
022249,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2016-12-13 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.
022250,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2016-12-14 MAS  Updated from comment-proofed Luminary 99 version.
022251,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2016-01-16 HG   Transcribed
022252,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-22 HG   Shift pseudo label +3 to column 2.
022253,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              Add missing operator INHINT
022254,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-23 HG   Fix operator CCS -> CA
022255,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix value TENDEG .27... -> .027...
022256,000025:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand R22LEM42 -> R22LEM
022257,000026:                                                                                                  ##                                          GOXDSPF  -> GOXDSPFR
022258,000027:                                                                                                  ##                                          BIT13    -> BIT3
022259,000028:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand modifier WWPOS +6 -> WWPOS +4
022260,000029:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix statement CA FLAGWRD2 -> CS FLAGWRD0
022261,000030:                                                                                                  ##                                            EXTEND      -> CCS A
022262,000031:                                                                                                  ##                                            BZF NOTP20  -> TC  NOTP20
022263,000032:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-27 RSB  Proofed comment text using octopus/prooferComments
022264,000033:                                                                                                  ##                              and fixed errors found.
022265,000034:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-28 RSB  WTIH -> WITH.
022266,000035: 
022267,000036:                                                                                                  ##

022269,000038: 
022270,000039:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022271,000040:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022272,000041:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022273,000042:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022274,000043:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022275,000044: 
022276,000045:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022277,000046:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
022278,000047:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022279,000048:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022280,000049:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022281,000050: 
022282,000051:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022283,000052:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022284,000053:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022285,000054:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022286,000055:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022287,000056:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022288,000057:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022289,000058:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022290,000059:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022291,000060:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022292,000061:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
022293,000062:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022294,000063:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022295,000064:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022296,000065:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022297,000066:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022298,000067:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022299,000068:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022300,000069:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022301,000070:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022302,000071:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022303,000072:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022304,000073:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022305,000074:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
022306,000075: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022307,000076: 
022308,000077: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
022309,000078: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022310,000079: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022311,000080: 
022312,000081: 24,2022  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022313,000082: 24,2022                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022314,000083: 24,2022  24,2022               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
022315,000084: 24,2022           05327        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG

022743,000512:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022744,000513:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022745,000514:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022746,000515:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022747,000516:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022748,000517: 
022749,000518:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022750,000519:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022751,000520:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022752,000521:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022753,000522:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022754,000523:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022755,000524:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022756,000525:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022757,000526:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022758,000527:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022759,000528:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022760,000529:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022761,000530:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022762,000531:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022763,000532:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022764,000533:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022765,000534:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022766,000535:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022767,000536:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022768,000537:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022769,000538:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

022818,000587:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022819,000588:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022820,000589:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022821,000590:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022822,000591:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022823,000592: 
022824,000593:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022825,000594:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022826,000595:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022827,000596:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022828,000597:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022829,000598:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022830,000599:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
022831,000600:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
022832,000601:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
022833,000602:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022834,000603:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022835,000604:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022836,000605:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
022837,000606:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-

023019,000788:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023020,000789:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023021,000790:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023022,000791:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023023,000792:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023024,000793: 
023025,000794:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023026,000795:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023027,000796:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023028,000797:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023029,000798:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
023030,000799:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023031,000800:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023032,000801:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
023033,000802:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
023034,000803:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023035,000804:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023036,000805:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023037,000806:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023038,000807:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023039,000808:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023040,000809:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023041,000810:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023042,000811:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023043,000812:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023044,000813:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023045,000814:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
023046,000815:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023047,000816:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
023048,000817:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023049,000818:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023050,000819: 24,2721  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023051,000820: 24,2721                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
023052,000821: 24,2721           32341        R21LEM             CAF      MAXTRIES                              #  ALLOW 60 PASSES (APPROX 45 SECS.) TO
023053,000822: 24,2722           55114                           TS       DESCOUNT                              #  DESIGNATE AND LOCKON
023054,000823: 24,2723           02714                           TC       LUNSFCHK                              
023055,000824: 24,2724           02731                           TC       R21LEM5

023130,000899:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM

023200,000969:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023201,000970:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023202,000971:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023203,000972:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023204,000973:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023205,000974: 
023206,000975:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023207,000976:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023208,000977:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023209,000978:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023210,000979:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023211,000980:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023212,000981:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023213,000982:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023214,000983:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023215,000984:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023216,000985:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023217,000986:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023218,000987:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023219,000988:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023220,000989:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023221,000990:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023222,000991:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023223,000992:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023224,000993:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023225,000994:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023226,000995:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023227,000996:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023228,000997:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023229,000998:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023230,000999: 24,3100  E7,1731                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023231,001000: 24,3100                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023232,001001: 24,3100           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
023233,001002: 24,3101           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
023234,001003: 24,3102           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023235,001004: 24,3103           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023236,001005: 24,3104           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO

023239,001008: 24,3107           55733                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

023497,001266:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023498,001267: 
023499,001268:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023500,001269:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023501,001270:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023502,001271:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023503,001272:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023504,001273:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023505,001274:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023506,001275:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023507,001276:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023508,001277:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023509,001278:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023510,001279:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023511,001280:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023512,001281:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023513,001282:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023514,001283: 
023515,001284:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023516,001285:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)

023521,001290:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023522,001291:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).

023577,001346:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023578,001347: 
023579,001348:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023580,001349:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023581,001350:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023582,001351:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023583,001352:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023584,001353:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023585,001354:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023586,001355:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023587,001356:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023588,001357:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023589,001358:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023590,001359:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023591,001360:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023592,001361:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023593,001362:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023594,001363:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023595,001364:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023596,001365:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023597,001366:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023598,001367:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023599,001368:

023648,001417:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023649,001418: 
023650,001419:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023651,001420: 
023652,001421:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023653,001422:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023654,001423:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023655,001424:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023656,001425:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023657,001426:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023658,001427:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023659,001428:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023660,001429:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023661,001430:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023662,001431:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023663,001432:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023664,001433: 
023665,001434:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023666,001435:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
023667,001436:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023668,001437: 
023669,001438:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023670,001439:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023671,001440: 
023672,001441:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023673,001442: 
023674,001443:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023675,001444:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023676,001445: 
023677,001446:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023678,001447: 
023679,001448:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023680,001449: 
023681,001450: 24,3151                                           BANK     24                                    
023682,001451: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023683,001452: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023684,001453: 
023685,001454: 25,2062  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023686,001455: 25,2062                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023687,001456: 25,2062           02071        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023688,001457: 25,2063           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023689,001458: 25,2064           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
023690,001459: 25,2065           44753                           CS       BIT1

023696,001465:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023697,001466: 
023698,001467:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023699,001468:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023700,001469:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023701,001470:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023702,001471:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023703,001472:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
023704,001473:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023705,001474:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023706,001475:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023707,001476:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023708,001477:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023709,001478:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023710,001479:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023711,001480:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023712,001481:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023713,001482:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023714,001483: 
023715,001484:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023716,001485:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023717,001486:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023718,001487: 
023719,001488:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023720,001489: 
023721,001490:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023722,001491:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023723,001492: 
023724,001493:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
023725,001494: 
023726,001495:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023727,001496: 
023728,001497: 25,2071           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
023729,001498: 25,2072           23315                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
023730,001499: 25,2073           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023731,001500: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023732,001501: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023733,001502: 25,2076           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023734,001503: 25,2077           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023735,001504: 
023736,001505: 25,2100           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
023737,001506: 25,2101           54035                           TS       CDUT                                  
023738,001507: 25,2102           54036                           TS       CDUS                                  
023739,001508: 25,2103           44753                           CS       ONE                                   #  REMOVE ZEROING BIT.
023740,001509: 25,2104           00006                           EXTEND

023770,001539:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023771,001540:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023772,001541:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023773,001542:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023774,001543:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023775,001544:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023776,001545:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023777,001546:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023778,001547:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023779,001548:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023780,001549:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023781,001550:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023782,001551:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023783,001552:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023784,001553:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023785,001554:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023786,001555:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
023787,001556:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
023788,001557:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
023789,001558:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023790,001559:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
023791,001560:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
023792,001561:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
023793,001562:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
023794,001563: 
023795,001564:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023796,001565:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
023797,001566:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
023798,001567: 
023799,001568:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023800,001569:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023801,001570: 
023802,001571:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023803,001572:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
023804,001573: 
023805,001574:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023806,001575:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023807,001576: 
023808,001577:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
023809,001578: 
023810,001579:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES

023859,001628:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023860,001629: 
023861,001630:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023862,001631:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
023863,001632:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023864,001633:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023865,001634:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023866,001635:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023867,001636:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023868,001637:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023869,001638:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023870,001639:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023871,001640:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023872,001641:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023873,001642:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
023874,001643:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023875,001644:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023876,001645:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
023877,001646:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023878,001647:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023879,001648:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
023880,001649:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023881,001650: 
023882,001651:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023883,001652:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023884,001653:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023885,001654:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023886,001655:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
023887,001656: 
023888,001657:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023889,001658:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023890,001659: 
023891,001660:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023892,001661:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023893,001662:

023895,001664:                                                                                                  #  NONE

023953,001722:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023954,001723: 
023955,001724:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023956,001725:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023957,001726:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
023958,001727:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023959,001728:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
023960,001729:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
023961,001730:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023962,001731:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023963,001732:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
023964,001733:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023965,001734:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
023966,001735:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023967,001736:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023968,001737:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023969,001738:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
023970,001739: 
023971,001740:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023972,001741:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
023973,001742:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
023974,001743:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023975,001744:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023976,001745: 
023977,001746:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023978,001747:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023979,001748: 
023980,001749:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023981,001750:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023982,001751: 
023983,001752:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023984,001753:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023985,001754: 
023986,001755:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023987,001756: 
023988,001757:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023989,001758:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)
023990,001759:                                                                                                  #  L+1  (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)

024042,001811:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024043,001812: 
024044,001813:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024045,001814:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024046,001815:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024047,001816:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024048,001817:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024049,001818:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024050,001819:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024051,001820:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024052,001821:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024053,001822:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024054,001823:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024055,001824:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024056,001825:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024057,001826:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024058,001827: 
024059,001828:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024060,001829:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024061,001830:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
024062,001831: 
024063,001832:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024064,001833:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
024065,001834:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
024066,001835: 
024067,001836:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024068,001837:                                                                                                  #  MAGSUB
024069,001838: 
024070,001839:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024071,001840:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024072,001841:

024148,001917:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
024149,001918: 
024150,001919:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024151,001920:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
024152,001921:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
024153,001922:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
024154,001923:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
024155,001924:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
024156,001925:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
024157,001926:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
024158,001927:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
024159,001928:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
024160,001929:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
024161,001930:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
024162,001931:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
024163,001932:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
024164,001933:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
024165,001934:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
024166,001935:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
024167,001936:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
024168,001937:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
024169,001938:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
024170,001939:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
024171,001940:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
024172,001941:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
024173,001942: 
024174,001943:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024175,001944:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
024176,001945:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
024177,001946:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024178,001947:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024179,001948: 
024180,001949:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024181,001950:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
024182,001951: 
024183,001952:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024184,001953:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
024185,001954:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
024186,001955: 
024187,001956:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024188,001957:                                                                                                  #     NONE
024189,001958: 
024190,001959:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024191,001960: 
024192,001961:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
024193,001962:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
024194,001963:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
024195,001964: 
024196,001965: 25,2373           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
024197,001966: 25,2374           01113                                    DESRET

024201,001970: 25,2377           47443                                    CDUTRIG                               
024202,001971: 25,2400           45175                           VLOAD    CALL                                  #  LOAD VECTOR AND CALL TRANSFORMATION
024203,001972: 25,2401           01102                                    RRTARGET                              
024204,001973: 25,2402           47575                                    *SMNB*

024207,001976: 25,2404           26133                                    RRANGLES                              #  ALTERNATE MODE.
024208,001977: 25,2405           77776                           EXIT
